FNV PBR VPT/NVR CONTRACT GAP AUDIT

Goal:
- Map vanilla close-land shader table slots to branch context.
- Check where VPT-style pass IDs, terrain constants, and row IDs appear in vanilla functions.
- Identify remaining static gaps before runtime instrumentation.
